### [87] [LLMs Can Better Capture Human Judgments--With the Right Prompts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12754)
*Danica Dillion,Chen Cecilia Liu,Baihui Wang,Daniele Barolo,Tanmay Rajore,Niket Tandon,Pranathi Ravikumar,Kurt Gray*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了大语言模型（LLMs）在捕捉人类判断方面的局限性，并提出简单的提示策略来改善其表现。通过两个数据集（美国代表性道德情景和覆盖32个国家的国际社会调查项目中的道德信念），研究发现，通过提示模型报告标准差和响应比例，能更好恢复人类响应的完整分布；同时，确保情景对人类清晰（基于人类困惑度评分）可显著提升模型与人类的一致性，且LLM能够跟踪人类的困惑度。尽管模型对自己的错误估计校准较差，但能较好预测人类的变异性。结论是：通过优化提问方式，可以显著提升LLM的回答质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在捕捉人类判断方面存在两大问题：一是无法充分反映人类响应的完整分布，二是对表述变化敏感，导致判断不稳定。这限制了其在涉及人类价值观和道德判断任务中的可靠性。因此需要探索改进方法以增强AI与人类判断的一致性。

Method: 采用两种简单提示策略：1）要求模型报告响应的标准差和比例，以更全面地捕捉人类响应分布；2）基于人类对情景的困惑度评分，筛选或重构情景以提高清晰度，进而评估模型在不同清晰度条件下的表现。使用两个大规模数据集验证方法的有效性，包括美国代表性道德场景和跨国家的道德信念数据。

Result: 提示模型报告标准差和响应比例显著提升了对人类响应分布的还原能力；提高情景清晰度后，模型与人类判断的一致性明显增强，且模型能有效跟踪人类的困惑度。然而，模型对其自身错误的估计缺乏良好校准，尽管其对人类变异性的预测能力较强。

Conclusion: 通过优化提示设计，如要求模型报告统计特征并确保情境清晰，可以显著提升大语言模型在捕捉人类道德判断方面的表现。这表明‘问得更好’能让‘答得更好’，为未来人机对齐研究提供了实用路径。

Abstract: Are large language models (LLMs) bad at capturing human judgment? Two commonly stated limitations are that LLMs fail to capture full distributions of responses, and that their judgments are unstable across wording variations. We demonstrate simple prompting strategies that mitigate these limitations. Across two datasets--a U.S.-representative set of 144 moral scenarios and 38 moral beliefs from the International Social Survey Programme's Family and Changing Gender Roles module covering 32 countries--we show how simple elicitation techniques help improve AI-human alignment. First, prompting models to report standard deviations and response proportions recovers the full range of human responses better than common strategies. Second, ensuring scenarios are clear to human participants--as reflected in human confusion ratings--boosts model alignment, and LLMs can track human confusion ratings. At the same time, we find that LLMs' estimates of their own error are poorly calibrated, though they can predict human variability relatively well. These results suggest that asking better questions to LLMs can yield better answers.

</details>


### [88] [Rigel: Reverse-Engineering the Metal 4.1 Tensor Compute Path on the Apple M4 Max GPU](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12765)
*Ramchand Kumaresan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Rigel empirically characterizes Apple's Metal 4.1's fp8 matmul2d operation on M4 Max, revealing it is emulated rather than hardware-accelerated, executes entirely on GPU shader cores, accumulates in >=fp32, and uses an 8x8 cooperative_tensor fragment layout. A hand-fused kernel achieves 6.5-12.9% better performance.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the hidden hardware behavior of Metal 4.1's matmul2d operation over cooperative_tensor fragments, which is documented but not transparently implemented.

Method: Using a checksum-gated, provenance-tracked microbenchmark harness with three-signal triangulation (throughput ceiling, simdgroup_matrix comparison, per-rail power attribution) to reverse-engineer the operation's execution path, accumulator width, and fragment layout.

Result: The fp8 matmul2d is emulated, not accelerated; it runs on GPU shader cores without Neural Engine involvement, accumulates in >=fp32, and uses an undocumented 8x8 fragment layout. A hand-fused kernel outperforms the decomposed path by 6.5-12.9%.

Conclusion: Metal 4.1's fp8 matmul2d is a memory-footprint feature, not a performance one on M4 Max; its behavior is fully emulated on GPU shader cores, and optimization requires low-level kernel fusion.

Abstract: Apple's Metal 4.1 exposes a tensor compute path: the Metal Performance Primitives (MPP) matmul2d operation over cooperative_tensor fragments, whose interface is documented but whose hardware behavior is deliberately hidden. The specification states which data-type rows are supported, never whether they are hardware-accelerated, where the operation physically executes, what its accumulator width is, or how it partitions matrix fragments across threads. We present Rigel, an empirical characterization of this path on a single Apple M4 Max (a pre-neural-accelerator generation). Using a checksum-gated, provenance-tracked microbenchmark harness, Rigel recovers eleven facts the v4.1 specification hides or contradicts. The headline finding: the Metal 4.1 fp8 (E4M3) matmul2d is emulated, not accelerated: it sustains 0.94x the throughput of fp16 despite reading half the operand bytes, so on M4 it is a memory-footprint feature, not a performance feature. We further show, via a three-signal triangulation (throughput ceiling, comparison against simdgroup_matrix, and per-rail power attribution), that matmul2d executes entirely on the GPU shader cores with no dedicated matrix datapath and no evidence of Apple Neural Engine routing; that it accumulates in >=fp32; and we reconstruct the opaque 8x8 cooperative_tensor fragment layout Apple documents nowhere. Acting on the characterization, a hand-fused GEMM + bias + GELU kernel beats the decomposed path by +6.5-12.9% in the cache-resident regime. All findings are reproducible from committed MIT-licensed code and per-cell CSVs.

</details>


### [89] [How Fine-Grained Should a RAG Benchmark Be? A Hierarchical Framework for Synthetic Question Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12789)
*Chase M. Fensore,Kaustubh Dhole,Jason Fan,Eugene Agichtein,Joyce C. Ho*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出HieraRAG，一个用于研究RAG评估基准构建中粒度的分层框架，定义最优粒度为在给定RAG配置下最大化生成质量差异性的水平。通过在三个维度（问题复杂度、答案类型、语言变化）上生成5,872个合成问答对，发现不同维度的最优粒度不同：问题复杂度适合细粒度（区分度0.053），而答案类型和语言变化则在中等粒度时表现最佳。引入Coherence Ratio指标衡量细粒度划分是否清晰，揭示了各维度结构差异。人类评估验证了合成数据质量。该方法可推广至不同RAG设置以确定合适评估粒度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前缺乏实证指导来决定在评估RAG系统时应如何变化问题特征及其粒度，因此需要一种系统化方法来确定最优评估基准的粒度水平。

Method: 提出分层框架HieraRAG，通过在三个维度上设计不同粒度（2、4、8类）的合成问答对，并使用BM25+Falcon-3-10B模型进行测试，结合标准差分析判别度与Coherence Ratio评估分类结构清晰性。

Result: 问题复杂度在细粒度下表现最佳（区分度0.053），而答案类型和语言变化在中等粒度下达到峰值；Coherence Ratio显示问题复杂度的划分较模糊（0.40），答案类型更清晰（1.44）。人类评估确认合成数据质量可靠。

Conclusion: HieraRAG提供了一种可迁移的方法和验证指标，使实践者能够在自身RAG设置中确定合适的评估粒度，尽管具体结果依赖于特定配置。

Abstract: Evaluating retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems requires benchmarks that capture diverse question characteristics, yet practitioners lack empirical guidance on which dimensions to vary and at what granularity. We present HieraRAG, a hierarchical framework for studying granularity in RAG benchmark construction, defining optimal granularity as the level that maximizes discriminative power (the standard deviation of generation quality across categories) within a given RAG configuration. As a case study, we generate 5,872 synthetic question-answer (QA) pairs from FineWeb-10BT across 3 dimensions (Question Complexity, Answer Type, Linguistic Variation) at 3 granularity levels (2, 4, and 8 categories). With a BM25+Falcon-3-10B pipeline, optimal granularity varies by dimension: complexity benefits from fine-grained distinctions (discriminative power: 0.053) while answer type and linguistic variation peak at medium granularity. We introduce a Coherence Ratio metric to quantify whether fine-grained splits cleanly subdivide parent categories, revealing structural differences across dimensions (Question Complexity: 0.40 vs. Answer Type: 1.44). Human evaluation of 110 stratified QA pairs confirms synthetic quality. While these specific findings reflect a single configuration, HieraRAG provides a portable procedure and validation metric for practitioners to determine evaluation granularity within their own RAG settings.

Result: 实验表明，传统整体性评估指标无法有效捕捉创新性的多维度特性，而GENIE能够精准识别创新性来源，并揭示不同缓解策略在提升创新性上的实际效果与局限。

Conclusion: GENIE为评估大语言模型在任务特定场景下的创新性提供了有效工具，有助于理解现有方法的不足并指导未来改进方向。

Abstract: Large Language Models have consistently demonstrated a lack of creativity and diversity across tasks. Here, we aim to consider novelty and investigate what makes model-generated content novel or not novel in a task-specific manner. We propose a fine-grained evaluation metric GENIE to measure the novelty of responses along task-specific features with respect to a population of responses. We show that unlike GENIE, holistic metrics struggle to capture the high-dimensionality of novelty and do not provide insight on which properties they target. Finally, we use GENIE to measure the effectiveness of mitigation methods that address creativity to better understand where these methods can improve novelty.

### [91] [Detect, Remask, Repair: Diffusion Editing for Faithful Summarization of Evolving Contexts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12807)
*Hao Zou,Zachary Horvitz,Chandhru Karthick,Zhou Yu,Kathleen McKeown*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于扩散模型的局部忠实度修复框架DETTECT-REMASK-REPAIR，用于在上下文演化时更新摘要中过时的部分，同时保留已支持的内容。通过引入StreamSum基准测试评估动态上下文摘要任务，实验表明该方法能有效减少修复成本（低于0.5秒），实现忠实度、速度与内容保留之间的权衡，并可作为自回归系统的事后修正步骤提升摘要质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有摘要在上下文变化时通常需要完全重写，导致信息丢失、难以追踪变更且效率低下；尤其当仅少数陈述过时的情况下，全量重写不必要且低效。因此需要一种能够精准定位并修复过时内容的方法。

Method: 提出DETTECT-REMASK-REPAIR框架：首先使用扩散模型识别摘要中过时的片段（detect），然后对这些部分进行掩码处理（remask），最后利用掩码扩散语言模型生成新的合理内容以修复（repair）。整个过程保持原有支持内容不变，实现局部更新。

Result: 在DialogSum和StreamSum数据集上的实验表明，该方法能以不到0.5秒的单步修复成本实现高质量更新；相比全量重写，显著提升了修复效率与可控性；同时可在不改变原始结构的前提下增强摘要的忠实度，适用于自回归系统的后处理修正。

Conclusion: 局部忠实度修复为动态环境下的摘要更新提供了一种高效、可控且可扩展的解决方案，能够在保证内容完整性的同时精确修复过时信息，具备实际应用价值。

Abstract: Summaries of real-world events can become outdated as contexts evolve and new information arrives. A common response is to generate a new summary from the updated context, but full regeneration discards the previous draft, can obscure what changed, and may be unnecessary when only a few claims are unsupported. We study localized faithfulness repair: updating outdated spans in an existing summary while preserving supported content. We propose DETECT-REMASK-REPAIR, a diffusion-based framework that identifies, remasks, and repairs outdated regions with masked diffusion language models. To evaluate evolving-context summarization, we introduce StreamSum, a benchmark of synthetic event timelines. Experiments on DialogSum and StreamSum show that localized diffusion repair provides a controllable alternative to full rewriting: faithfulness-steered repair improves early drafts, one-step repair reduces repair cost to under half a second, with the framework enabling faithfulness-speed-preservation tradeoffs across datasets. We also find that the framework can provide a post-hoc correction step that improves faithfulness for autoregressive systems.

### [92] [Localizing Anchoring Pathways in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12818)

TL;DR: 研究发现提示中的无关数字会引发语言模型的锚定效应，通过设计多选题实验和对数几率差度量验证了该现象。利用基于归因的电路定位方法，在7B-8B规模的Qwen与Llama模型中发现边缘级方法比节点级方法更准确地恢复锚定信号。低锚定与高锚定路径在模型内部具有强可转移性，表明存在共享的路径结构；但基础模型与指令微调模型之间的传递较弱，说明后训练阶段改变了关键路径。整体结果揭示了锚定相关决策信号在语言模型内部的机制性承载方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究语言模型在数值推理中受无关数字影响的锚定效应，理解其内部信号的承载机制。

Method: 采用控制变量的多选题实验，定义对数几率差度量以追踪锚定行为；使用归因驱动的电路定位技术分析7B-8B规模的Qwen与Llama模型（包括基础与指令微调版本）。

Result: 边缘级归因方法能更准确恢复锚定信号；低/高锚定路径在模型内具有强可转移性，显示共享路径结构；但基础模型与指令微调模型间转移能力弱，表明后训练过程影响关键路径选择。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了语言模型中锚定相关决策信号的机制性解释，揭示了信号在模型内部的路径结构与动态变化规律。

Abstract: Irrelevant numbers in a prompt can shift language model judgments, producing anchoring effects in numerical reasoning. We study where this anchor-sensitive signal is carried inside language models using a controlled multiple-choice setup with shared answer options. We define a logit-difference metric comparing the correct answer option with the answer option corresponding to the anchor, and validate that it tracks behavioral anchoring. Using attribution-based circuit localization on 7B--8B Qwen and Llama base and instruction-tuned models, we find that edge-level methods recover this signal more faithfully than node-level methods. Low- and high-anchor circuits transfer strongly within a model, suggesting shared pathway structure across anchor direction. However, sparse transfer across base and instruction-tuned variants is less reliable, indicating that post-training changes which pathways matter most. Overall, our results provide a mechanistic account of how anchoring-related decision signals are carried inside language models.

Method: 基于覆盖700万维基百科实体的知识图谱，通过自动选择具有大搜索空间的关系并组装成结构复杂的多跳问题，构建出544个经人工验证的高质量问题，确保答案唯一且可知识图谱验证。

To address this, we introduce LoHoSearch (Long-Horizon Search Agents), a challenging benchmark comprising 544 human-verified questions across 11 domains. LoHoSearch is constructed via an automated pipeline built upon a knowledge graph covering over 7 million Wikipedia entities, which selects relations with large search spaces and assembles them into structurally complex questions with KG-verified unique answers. Our evaluation demonstrates that even the strongest model achieves only 34.74% accuracy, and existing context management strategies (best +6.8%) yield far smaller gains than on prior benchmarks. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在组织文档检索中广泛应用，但基于自由重写的检索增强生成（RAG）系统易引入幻觉且在完整性和简洁性之间存在不稳定权衡，尤其在安全与合规关键场景下风险更高。因此需要一种更具抗幻觉能力的替代方案。

Method: 比较多种提示策略，包括基于行号的源选择、带显式安全标注的相关指南句子提取，以及利用支持证据对草稿答案进行多阶段精炼的管道方法。实验涵盖不同长度与结构的文档，包括英国国家健康服务体系（NHS）急症护理与肿瘤学指南及英国国家卫生与临床优化研究所（NICE）指南，使用前沿级与本地可部署模型进行测试。

Result: 基于行号的选择策略表现最优，在大模型与小模型上均优于直接复制和安全导向策略，实现高达95%的术语召回率，并与原始文本高度一致；安全导向方法虽提高精确度，但造成系统性遗漏；多阶段过滤进一步放大该权衡。文档结构影响结果：线性抽取在流程型内容中表现优异，其他策略在较冗长文档中效果更佳（最高达97%术语召回率）。

Conclusion: 线性抽取是一种高效且抗幻觉的RAG替代方案，尤其适用于结构化强的指南文档；不同文档类型需匹配相应策略以平衡精度、召回与安全性，未来应针对文档特征设计自适应抽取机制。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to access organisational documentation, including standard operating procedures (SOPs), HR policies and institutional guidelines. However, retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems that rely on free-form rewriting can introduce hallucinations and unstable trade-offs between completeness and conciseness, particularly in safety- and compliance-critical settings. Objectives: To evaluate extraction as a hallucination-resistant alternative to rewriting-based RAG and compare strategies that balance precision, recall and safety across document types and model scales. Methods: We compare multiple prompting strategies, including line-number-based source selection, extraction of relevant guideline sentences with explicit safety annotations, and a multi-stage pipeline that refines draft answers using supporting evidence from source guidelines. Experiments are conducted on documents of varying length and structure, including local NHS acute care and oncology guidelines and UK-wide NICE guidelines, using both frontier-scale and locally deployable models. Performance is assessed using automatic metrics and human expert evaluation of relevance and completeness. Results: Line-number selection achieves the strongest results, outperforming direct copying and safety-focused strategies across both large and small models while maintaining high term recall (up to 95%) and close alignment with source text. Safety-oriented approaches improve precision but introduce systematic omissions, while multi-stage filtering further amplifies this trade-off. Performance varies with document structure: line-based extraction excels in protocol-like content, whereas alternative strategies perform better on more verbose documents (up to 97% term recall).

### [97] [PRISM: Prosody-Integrated Multi-Agent Reasoning Framework for Empathetic Spoken Dialogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12902)
*Wen Zhang,Xiaocui Yang,Zhuoyue Gao,Shi Feng,Daling Wang,Yifei Zhang*

TL;DR: PRISM is a multi-agent framework for empathetic spoken dialogue that decouples speech perception, response generation, and speech synthesis. Conclusion: PRISM effectively enhances empathetic spoken dialogue by integrating emotional prosody and external knowledge through a modular, interpretable framework, demonstrating strong performance in both naturalness and empathy.

Abstract: Empathetic spoken dialogue systems require not only semantically appropriate responses but also emotionally aligned prosodic expression. However, cascade pipelines often discard acoustic cues during speech-to-text conversion, while end-to-end speech models lack interpretable control over emotion and knowledge integration. To address these challenges, we propose PRISM, a multi-agent framework for empathetic spoken dialogue that decouples speech perception, response generation, and speech synthesis into coordinated components. PRISM introduces a prosody-to-language translation mechanism to stabilize large language model reasoning and enables on-demand invocation of external knowledge tools for empathetic dialogue generation. Experimental results demonstrate that PRISM achieves consistent improvements in empathy, prosodic appropriateness, and text response generation quality across objective and subjective metrics. Our code is available at: https://github.com/Bxzfrm/PRISM.

### [98] [X-MADAM-RAG: Diagnosing and Handling Chinese-English Evidence Conflict in Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12903)
*Yongqi Kang,Yu Fu,Yong Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究针对多语言RAG系统中检索到的相互矛盾证据问题，提出X-RAMDocs-ZHEN基准和X-MADAM-RAG可解释流水线。在受控基准上，X-MADAM-RAG表现优异，但在自然化压力测试中性能大幅下降，表明文档级提取是主要瓶颈。研究强调该工具用于诊断证据冲突而非通用幻觉检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多语言RAG系统常面临中英文检索证据之间的矛盾，影响答案准确性，亟需有效诊断与处理机制。

Method: 构建X-RAMDocs-ZHEN多语言对比基准，设计X-MADAM-RAG流水线，包含候选提取、可见证据修复、确定性分组与冲突感知聚合，并通过规则提取器与自然化压力测试评估其鲁棒性。

Result: 在受控基准上X-MADAM-RAG严格准确率达0.9667，但自然化测试中降至0.3000，远低于基线；规则提取器在无模板时失效，表明模型依赖显式模板而非真实理解。

Conclusion: X-RAMDocs-ZHEN与X-MADAM-RAG是诊断证据冲突的有效工具，但不能代表对自然检索或幻觉的普遍鲁棒性，核心挑战在于文档级信息提取能力不足。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems may receive evidence that is not merely noisy but mutually contradictory. This issue becomes particularly salient in multilingual settings, where retrieved Chinese and English evidence may support incompatible answer candidates. We study this problem through X-RAMDocs-ZHEN, a controlled Chinese-English benchmark derived from RAMDocs for diagnosing evidence conflict in RAG. The benchmark contains 300 examples across six balanced conditions, including monolingual support, bilingual agreement, reversed conflict directions, and conflict with optional noise. We further examine X-MADAM-RAG, an interpretable pipeline that decomposes evidence handling into per-document candidate extraction, visible-evidence repair, deterministic candidate grouping, and conflict-aware aggregation. On the original controlled benchmark with Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct, X-MADAM-RAG achieves 0.9667 strict accuracy and 0.9767 conflict-aware success, outperforming an evidence-normalized single-call baseline. However, a zero-call rule-only extractor reaches 1.0000 on the same benchmark, revealing strong template regularity. To probe this limitation, we construct a deterministic naturalized stress test that removes explicit answer templates while preserving candidate strings. On its 100-sample subset, rule-only extraction falls to 0.0000, but X-MADAM-RAG also drops to 0.3000 strict accuracy, below both naive and evidence-normalized baselines. A privileged oracle remains perfect, indicating that document-level extraction is the main bottleneck. These findings position X-RAMDocs-ZHEN and X-MADAM-RAG as diagnostic tools for controlled evidence conflict rather than as evidence of general hallucination detection or robustness to natural retrieval.

### [99] [SENTINEL: Failure-Driven Reinforcement Learning for Training Tool-Using Language Model Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12908)
*Ziyi Wang,Yuxuan Lu,Yimeng Zhang,Qun Liu,Chen Luo,Jiri Gesi,Hanqing Lu,Yisi Sang,Manling Li,Jing Huang,Dakuo Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SENTINEL是一种基于失败驱动的强化学习框架，通过将智能体的失败轨迹转化为针对性的训练任务，提升工具使用语言模型代理的可靠性。它采用控制器-提议者-求解器循环：控制器分析失败模式，提议者生成针对弱点的任务，求解器在这些任务上进行训练。在Tau2-Bench Retail上，SENTINEL将Pass^1从66.4提升至74.9，并在多种指标上优于传统强化学习方法，证明了模型失败可作为有效且可扩展的训练信号来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前训练可靠的工具使用语言模型代理仍具挑战性，尤其是当任务固定时，任务分布与策略能力不匹配，导致大量无效探索。如何高效利用失败信息以生成有意义的训练任务成为关键问题。

Method: SENTINEL采用控制器-提议者-求解器循环：控制器分析失败轨迹并提取常见错误模式；提议者根据这些模式生成具有挑战性的新任务；求解器在这些针对性任务上进行强化学习训练，从而持续改进性能。

Result: 在Tau2-Bench Retail数据集上，SENTINEL将Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507模型的Pass^1从66.4提升至74.9，并在Pass^k各项指标上优于传统强化学习方法，验证了其有效性与泛化能力。

Conclusion: 模型失败不仅是问题，更是宝贵的训练信号。SENTINEL通过系统性地挖掘和利用失败，实现了对工具使用语言模型代理的持续优化，为构建更可靠、自适应的智能体提供了新范式。

Abstract: Language model agents are increasingly effective in solving realistic tasks through multi-turn tool use. However, training reliable tool-using agents remains challenging in practice. While reinforcement learning provides an on-policy paradigm for improving agents from their own environment interactions, its effectiveness depends heavily on the training task distribution. When tasks are fixed before training, the task distribution can become increasingly mismatched with the policy's evolving capabilities, causing many rollouts to be spent on uninformative tasks. We propose SENTINEL, a failure-driven reinforcement learning framework that turns the Solver's rollout failures into targeted training tasks. SENTINEL follows a Controller--Proposer--Solver loop: the Controller analyzes failed trajectories and summarizes recurring error patterns, the Proposer generates executable tasks that stress these weaknesses, and the Solver is trained on the targeted tasks. On Tau2-Bench Retail with Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507, SENTINEL improves Pass\^{}1 from 66.4 to 74.9 and outperforms RL on general synthetic tasks across Pass\^{}k metrics. These results demonstrate that model failures provide an effective and scalable source of targeted training signal for improving tool-using language model agents.

</details>


### [100] [PiDA: Phonetically-Informed Data Augmentation for Robust Vietnamese Speech Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12911)
*Giang Son Nguyen,Tung X. Nguyen,Hieu Minh Truong,Nhu Vo,Wray Buntine,Dung D. Le*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文针对越南语语音翻译（ST）系统中因自动语音识别（ASR）错误导致的误差传播问题，首次对越南语ASR错误进行了系统分类，按发音原因划分替换错误，并通过线性混合效应模型量化其对神经机器翻译（NMT）性能的影响。研究发现，大多数ASR替换错误源于发音混淆而非随机噪声，且显著降低ST质量。为此，提出一种基于发音信息的数据增强方法PiDA，通过使用发音词嵌入将词语替换为发音相似的替代词来生成类似ASR的噪声。在FLEURS越南语-英语数据集上微调时，PiDA显著提升了对错误ASR输出的翻译性能（最高提升2.04 BLEU），同时轻微改善了干净文本的翻译效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ASR错误会引发语音翻译系统中的误差传播问题，尤其在越南语场景下缺乏对错误类型和影响的系统分析。因此需要理解并缓解由发音混淆引起的错误对下游翻译任务的影响。

Method: 提出基于发音信息的数据增强方法PiDA，利用发音词嵌入模拟实际ASR中常见的发音混淆错误，生成带有音似替换的合成噪声数据，用于模型微调。

Result: 在FLEURS越南语-英语数据集上，采用PiDA增强后的模型在处理错误ASR输出时，翻译性能最高提升2.04 BLEU；同时在干净文本上也略有提升。

Conclusion: 发音混淆是越南语ASR错误的主要来源，其对语音翻译质量有显著负面影响。通过引入发音感知的数据增强方法PiDA，可有效提升模型对错误输入的鲁棒性，同时保持或提升整体翻译性能。

Abstract: Cascaded speech translation (ST) systems suffer from error propagation when Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) outputs incorrect transcripts. We present the first systematic categorization of ASR errors for Vietnamese ST, classifying substitution errors by phonetic cause and quantifying their impact on downstream Neural Machine Translation (NMT) performance using Linear Mixed-Effects Modelling. We confirm that most ASR substitution errors arise from phonetic confusions rather than random noise, and that these phonetic errors significantly degrade ST quality. Motivated by this finding, we propose Phonetically-Informed Data Augmentation (PiDA), which generates ASR-like corruptions by substituting words with phonetically similar alternatives using phonetic word embeddings. Fine-tuning on a PiDA-augmented version of FLEURS Vietnamese-English improves translation of erroneous ASR outputs (up to +2.04 BLEU over standard fine-tuning) while also slightly improving clean-text performance.

### [101] [Polar: A Benchmark for Evaluating Political Bias in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12922)

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Polar 是一个包含 4,026 个实例的多项选择基准，通过选项级似然性而非基于提示的生成来衡量大语言模型的政治偏见。该基准涵盖两个意识形态轴和八个议题类别，评估模型在美韩政治语境下的表现。研究发现，所有模型在美国政治内容上均偏向左翼进步派，但在韩国内容上呈现更中立或混合模式；语言呈现方式本身也会影响测量到的偏见。结果强调了跨语言、跨情境评估大模型政治偏见的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建 Polar 基准，采用选项级似然性分析，覆盖美国与韩国政治语境，评估 38 个 LLM 在多个议题类别上的表现，并进行翻译实验以考察语言呈现的影响。

Result: 模型在美式政治内容中普遍偏向左翼，而在韩式内容中表现更中立或多样；语言呈现可显著改变测得的偏见水平。

Conclusion: 政治偏见在大语言模型中具有高度上下文依赖性，必须在多语言、跨文化环境中进行系统评估，以确保公平性和可靠性。

Abstract: Political bias in large language models (LLMs) is increasingly significant, but difficult to measure reproducibly across political and linguistic contexts. We introduce Polar, a 4,026-instance multiple-choice benchmark that measures political bias through option-level likelihoods rather than prompt-based generation. Polar covers two ideological axes and eight issue categories derived from the Manifesto Project, and evaluates models in parallel across U.S. and South Korean political contexts. Across 38 LLMs, measured bias varies systematically with political context, issue category, model group, and presentation language. All models lean left-progressive on U.S. political content, but show more centered and mixed patterns on South Korean content. Translation experiments further show that presentation language alone can shift measured bias. These findings highlight the need for multilingual and cross-contextual evaluation of political bias in LLMs.

### [102] [Multi-Turn Reasoning When Context Arrives in Pieces: Scalable Sharding and Memory-Augmented RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12941)
*Shu Tong Luo,Wenqin Liu,Rui Liu,Mingming Gong,Jiaxian Guo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出通过训练模型维护紧凑的滚动记忆来缓解多轮对话中的信息丢失问题，使用低成本分片管道将单轮问答数据转化为多轮碎片化信息场景，仅在sharded GSM8K上训练即可显著提升多轮任务准确率，并在零样本情况下泛化到更难的数学题和跨领域长上下文问答。即使在测试时提供完整历史，记忆增强模型仍优于依赖全历史的基线，表明学习压缩能带来比单纯暴露全上下文更鲁棒的增量推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当用户在多个对话轮次中逐步透露任务关键信息时，尽管上下文完整可用，大型语言模型的准确性会下降高达65%，这种现象称为'Lost in Conversation'。现有方法难以有效应对这一问题，因此需要一种能够持续维护关键信息、避免信息淹没的新机制。

Method: 引入一种低开销的分片流水线，将单轮问答数据集（如GSM8K）转换为包含碎片化信息的多轮对话场景；训练模型采用紧凑的滚动记忆机制，而非直接关注不断增长的历史记录，从而实现高效的信息保留与推理。

Result: 在仅使用sharded GSM8K进行训练后，模型在多轮任务上的准确率显著提升，并能在零样本条件下泛化至更复杂的数学问题和跨领域的长上下文问答任务；即便在测试阶段提供完整历史，其表现仍优于传统全历史处理模型。

Conclusion: 学习如何压缩和维护关键信息的滚动记忆，比单纯依赖完整上下文更能促进鲁棒的增量推理。该方法不仅提升了多轮对话性能，还具备良好的可扩展性和泛化能力。

Abstract: When a user reveals task-critical information across several conversation turns, LLM accuracy drops by up to 65% despite full context availability. We show that this Lost in Conversation degradation can be substantially mitigated by training models to maintain a compact rolling memory instead of attending to a growing history. To make such training scalable, we introduce a low-cost sharding pipeline that converts single-turn QA datasets into multi-turn fragmented-information episodes, eliminating the need for hours of manual annotation. Training only on sharded GSM8K, our memory-augmented policy significantly improves multi-turn accuracy and generalises zero-shot to harder math and out-of-domain long-context QA. Moreover, memory-trained models outperform full-history baselines even when given the full history at test time, suggesting that learning to compress induces more robust incremental reasoning than full-context exposure alone.

### [103] [SkillChain: Closing the Loop on Skill Evolution for Image-Based E-Commerce AI Assistants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12984)
*Yimin Hu,Mengtao Xu,Hao Guo,Yuheng Song,Xiaoyong Zhu,Bo Zheng*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于 LLM 的图像助手在面对多样化用户意图（如商品搜索、风格推荐等）时，因缺乏针对具体意图的行为约束，导致响应质量下降；而意图空间的广度和动态性使得手动工程不可行，亟需自动化解决方案。

Method: SkillChain 包含三个核心组件：Skill Creator 从任务规范和轨迹中初始化技能；Route Optimizer 实现意图路由对齐；Body Refiner 通过双路径 LLM-判别器评估进行迭代优化，形成闭环反馈机制。

Conclusion: SkillChain 成功实现了技能演化的自动化闭环，为大规模多意图 AI 助手提供了可扩展、可维护的解决方案，具有显著的实际应用价值。

Without per-intent behavioral constraints, LLM-based systems conflate these heterogeneous modes and fall short of domain quality standards, while the breadth and dynamism of the intent space render manual engineering infeasible. To address this, we present SkillChain, which closes the production feedback loop on Skill evolution, automating the lifecycle of Skills through three stages: Skill Creator for bootstrapping from task specs and trajectories, Route Optimizer for routing alignment, and Body Refiner for iterative Skill Body refinement via dual-path LLM-Judge evaluation. Deployed on a production-scale e-commerce image assistant, SkillChain substantially improves aggregate response quality, with the strongest gains on structural compliance and content quality; a one-week online A/B experiment further confirms significant gains in user engagement, content consumption, and long-term retention.

### [104] [No Hidden Prompts Needed! You Can Game AI Peer Review with Presentation-Only Revisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13044)
*Xu Yang,Zhizhou Sha,Junbo Li,Jian Yu,Yifan Sun,Matthew Zhao,Jinrui Fang,Xinyue Guo,Yining Wu,Xu Hu,Yifu Luo,Qiang Liu,Zhangyang Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究AI生成评审在无隐藏指令、无提示注入等显式攻击下的隐性失败模式，提出‘对抗性再包装’攻击：仅修改论文的呈现内容（如摘要、贡献框架、相关工作、讨论和叙事结构），利用AI评审反馈进行闭环优化。在三个主流AI评审器上，该攻击成功率达75.1%，平均得分提升1.21/10，且效果不源于普通语言润色。分析发现，改变评审者对论文的理解策略（如重新定位相关工作、扩展分析讨论）远优于表面修改（如润色、表格格式调整）。揭示两大深层缺陷：AI评审更易被强调优点所打动，而试图化解弱点常适得其反；且容易将‘看似解决局限’误认为‘真正解决’，导致未变证据被重新解读为更强贡献。研究警示：论文呈现本身正成为可被优化的新攻击面，而非仅限于恶意指令。作者发布免污染滚动基准与攻击框架，用于测试AI评审是否仍锚定于科学内容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对AI评审系统的鲁棒性研究多聚焦于显式攻击（如隐藏指令、提示注入），但忽略了更隐蔽、更具政策意义的失败模式——即攻击者仅通过修改论文的呈现层面内容（如摘要、叙述结构、相关工作布局）即可显著提升评审评分，而科学证据本身未作改动。这种攻击方式更难检测，且直接影响学术评价公正性。

Method: 提出对抗性再包装（adversarial repackaging）攻击框架：基于AI评审反馈，采用闭环搜索策略，在不改变实验、图表、公式、数值结果等科学内容的前提下，仅优化论文的表述与结构。通过迭代生成与评估，寻找能最大化提升评审分数的呈现修改方案。使用三个主流AI评审工具进行测试，并对比不同修改策略的效果。

Result: 对抗性再包装在三个主流AI评审系统中实现75.1%的攻击成功率，平均得分提升1.21分（满分10分）。该提升无法通过常规语言润色解释。其中，改变评审理解策略（如重述相关工作、扩展分析讨论）的策略效果显著优于表面格式优化。

Conclusion: AI评审系统存在结构性脆弱：它们更容易被‘呈现上的优势’所影响，而非真正的科学论证。论文的外观和叙事方式已成为可被优化的攻击面。未来需建立更稳健的评审机制，确保系统始终锚定于科学内容本身，而非形式表达。研究团队发布了可用于持续评估的免污染基准与攻击框架。

Abstract: As AI-generated reviews move from experimental tools into peer-review infrastructure, most robustness concerns have focused on explicit attacks such as hidden instructions and prompt injection. We study a harder and more policy-relevant failure mode: no hidden text, no prompt injection, and no changes to methods, experiments, figures, equations, proofs, or numerical results. The attacker modifies only presentation-level content, such as the abstract, contribution framing, related work, discussion, and narrative structure. We introduce adversarial repackaging: a closed-loop attack that uses AI-reviewer feedback to search for presentation-level revisions while keeping the scientific evidence fixed. Across three mainstream AI reviewers, adversarial repackaging achieves a 75.1% attack success rate and a mean score gain of +1.21/10. The effect is not explained by ordinary prose polishing. We also reveal that strategies that change how the reviewer interprets the paper, such as related-work repositioning and analytical discussion expansion, substantially outperform surface edits such as local polishing, table formatting, and algorithm boxes.
  Our analysis reveals two deeper structural failure modes. First, AI reviewers are easier to impress than to convince: highlighting strengths reliably increases perceived merit, while attempts to dissolve weaknesses frequently backfire. Second, AI reviewers can confuse the appearance of addressing a limitation with actually resolving it, allowing unchanged evidence to be reinterpreted as stronger scientific contribution. These results show that the deployment risk is not only malicious hidden instructions, but the emergence of paper presentation itself as an optimization surface. We release a contamination-free rolling benchmark and attack framework for testing whether AI reviewers remain anchored to scientific content under presentation-only edits.

</details>


### [105] [sebis at CRF Filling 2026: A Two-Stage Local LLM Pipeline for Medical CRF Filling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13082)

Method: 提出两阶段本地化架构：第一阶段进行二元存在性分类，第二阶段执行值提取；采用针对具体项目的少量示例上下文学习，不依赖外部API或模型微调，确保输出确定性和对文本证据的严格遵循。

Conclusion: 本研究展示了隐私保护、本地部署的LLM流程能够实现接近专有前沿模型的性能，为临床自然语言处理提供了可信赖、数据主权可控的实用范式。

Abstract: The extraction of structured clinical information from unstructured EHR notes is a persistent bottleneck in healthcare informatics. While large language models (LLMs) offer high performance, their deployment in clinical settings is hindered by privacy risks, inference costs, and the tendency to hallucinate beyond textual evidence. We address these challenges for the CL4Health 2026 Case Report Form (CRF) filling task by proposing a fully local, domain-adapted pipeline using the MedGemma-27B model. Our two-stage architecture, which separates binary presence classification from value extraction, enforces strict adherence to textual evidence and ensures deterministic outputs for negated, uncertain, or unknown states. By leveraging item-specific, few-shot in-context learning without external API calls or fine-tuning, our approach achieves a macro-F1 score of 0.55 on the official English test track. This result secures second place among all locally-hosted, open-source submissions. Our work demonstrates that privacy-preserving, on-premise LLM pipelines can achieve near-competitive performance with proprietary frontier models, providing a practical, data-sovereign framework for clinical NLP.

### [106] [LEDGER: A Long-Context Benchmark of Corporate Annual Reports for Grounded Financial Retrieval and Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13100)
*Charles Moslonka,Amaury de Vitry,Arthur Garnier,Hicham Randrianarivo,Emmanuel Malherbe*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LEDGER 是一个包含 4,999 份数字化企业年报的语料库，涵盖图文并茂的完整文档，用于评估大语言模型在长上下文场景下的金融信息提取与检索能力。该数据集提供 31 个财务关键绩效指标（KPI）的标注，并关联市场反应，构建了三个覆盖不同难度的评估基准：页面级 KPI 检索、对话式“大海捞针”单值查找和全量 KPI 提取任务。同时提供高质量人工标注、标注一致性评估及完整的工具链。案例研究还展示了董事长信件修辞与市场反应之间的关联性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建 LEDGER 语料库，包含完整的年度报告（含图表与叙述），为每份报告标注 31 个核心财务指标，并记录其在财报发布日后的市场反应。基于此构建三类评估任务：基于 TREC 风格的相关性判断的页面级检索任务、对话式单值查找任务、以及端到端的财务指标提取任务。同时提供人工 OCR 标注、标注者间一致性分析及自动化评估工具链。

Result: LEDGER 数据集成功支持了多种复杂任务的评估，验证了大语言模型在长文档中进行精确信息提取与推理的能力。案例研究表明，董事长信件的语言风格可有效预测市场反应，凸显了该数据集在深入分析非结构化文本与市场行为关系方面的潜力。

Conclusion: LEDGER 为金融领域的大语言模型评估提供了高保真、多维度、可扩展的基准，有助于推动模型在真实商业环境中的可靠性与实用性发展。

Abstract: Finance reporting is a natural proving ground for large language models, and the very-long-context capabilities of recent models across all sizes make rigorous evaluation in this domain an increasingly pressing need. Yet most public financial resources reduce the task to plain-text SEC 10-K filings paired with a handful of question-answer items. We release LEDGER (Long-context Evaluation of Documents for Grounded Extraction and Retrieval), a corpus of 4,999 digitized corporate annual reports - full documents with figures, tables, and narrative, not just regulatory filings. Each report is labeled with 31 consolidated financial KPIs to be extracted and linked to the market's reaction at the earnings date. From this data we derive three evaluation benchmarks spanning the difficulty spectrum: a pure page-level KPI retrieval task with TREC-style relevance judgments over 118,048 questions in natural language, a conversational "needle-in-a-haystack" single-value lookup, and a full KPI extraction task, both from long, numerically dense reports. We additionally provide human OCR-quality annotations with inter-annotator agreement and the complete extraction, validation, and scoring toolchain. We further demonstrate the dataset's research utility with a case study linking CEO-letter rhetoric to post-publication market impact.

### [107] [MÖVE: A Holistic LLM Benchmark for the German Public Sector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13111)
*Camilla Dalerci,Thilo Michael,Robin Schaefer,Daniel Weinland*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MÖVE 是一个针对德国公共部门的大型语言模型（LLM）综合评估基准，旨在解决现有评估基准在语言、地域和评估维度上的局限性。该基准评估了39个模型在性能（如摘要、问答、主题提取）和治理（如幻觉倾向、能耗、供应商透明度、与德国宪法价值及政党立场的一致性）两个维度的表现，并使用10个德语数据集进行多指标评估。结果显示，没有单一模型在所有任务中表现最优，模型大小并非质量的可靠预测指标。研究还验证了基准本身的可靠性与有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM评估基准多为英语或美国中心，且仅关注任务性能，无法满足德国公共部门对模型选择的特定需求，因此需要一个更全面、本地化的评估框架。

Method: 采用性能与治理双重维度评估，结合经典NLP指标、基于嵌入的方法以及大模型作为裁判的评估策略；构建了多个金标准与银标准德语数据集，涵盖公共行政领域。

Result: 无模型在所有指标上均领先；模型表现因任务而异，模型规模不能有效预测性能；基准具备良好统计精度与鲁棒性，评估结果可靠。

Conclusion: MÖVE是一个持续发展的动态基准，可为德国公共部门提供科学、全面的模型评估支持，其结果公开可查。

Abstract: We present MÖVE (Modelle für die Öffentliche Verwaltung Evaluieren), a holistic benchmark for evaluating large language models (LLMs) in the context of the German public sector. While LLMs are increasingly adopted in public administration, model selection remains largely ad hoc, and existing benchmarks offer limited guidance: they are predominantly English-centric, US-centric in content, and focus exclusively on task performance. MÖVE addresses these gaps by evaluating 39 models across two complementary dimensions. Performance criteria cover summarization, question answering, and topic extraction. Governance criteria assess hallucination tendencies, energy consumption, provider transparency, and alignment with German constitutional values and knowledge about positions by German political parties. In total, we utilize ten German-language datasets, including gold- and silverstandard datasets that we constructed to reflect public-administration domains. We employ a multi-metric evaluation strategy combining classical NLP metrics, embedding-based methods, and LLM-as-a-judge approaches. Our results show that no single model dominates across all criteria: top performers differ between tasks, and model size alone is a poor predictor of quality. We further evaluate the benchmark itself, analyzing its statistical precision, LLM judge reliability, the impact of our private datasets on model rankings, the sensitivity of our results to prompt formulation, and the validity of our energy consumption estimates. MÖVE is designed as a living benchmark under active development; results are publicly available at https://moeve.bundesdruckerei.de/.

*Minjun Choi,Yoonjin Jang,Sangwon Youn,Youngjoong Ko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: G-Long 是一种图增强框架，利用微调的小型语言模型（sLM）进行结构化三元组提取和关联检索，结合注意力感知的重要性评分机制，有效提升长对话中记忆的一致性和响应质量，显著降低计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在长对话系统中面临长期一致性挑战，主要由于长上下文推理能力不足以及处理大量原始文本的效率低下；传统方法依赖非结构化记忆存储易导致信息丢失，或使用计算成本高的大模型带来高延迟。

Method: 提出 G-Long 框架，采用微调的小型语言模型进行结构化三元组提取与关联检索，并引入基于 T5 摘要器交叉注意力信号的注意力感知重要性评分机制，以识别关键记忆。

Conclusion: G-Long 通过结构化记忆管理和高效注意力机制，在保证高性能的同时显著降低资源消耗，是实现长期一致性对话系统的有效解决方案。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) have advanced open-domain dialogue systems, maintaining long-term consistency remains a challenge due to inherent limitations in long-context reasoning and the inefficiency of processing extensive raw text. Existing approaches typically rely on either unstructured memory storage, which is prone to information loss, or computationally expensive LLMs that incur high latency. To address these limitations, we propose G-Long, a graph-enhanced framework that utilizes a fine-tuned small Language Model (sLM) for structured triplet extraction and associative retrieval, significantly reducing operational costs. Furthermore, we introduce the novel attention-aware importance scoring mechanism that leverages the intrinsic cross-attention signals of a T5 summarizer to identify salient memories. Extensive experiments across diverse benchmarks demonstrate that G-Long achieves state-of-the-art performance in both response generation and memory retrieval, yielding performance gains of up to 9.8% in response quality on MSC and 40.8% in retrieval recall on LME, while significantly minimizing computational overhead.

### [109] [EvoBrowseComp: Benchmarking Search Agents on Evolving Knowledge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13120)
*Yunhan Wang,Jiaan Wang,Lianzhe Huang,Xianfeng Zeng,Fandong Meng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: EvoBrowseComp 是一个动态更新的复杂问答基准，通过三代理协作框架从实时网络中自动合成400个英文和400个中文的无污染问题，旨在解决现有基准因静态知识导致的测试集污染与参数记忆问题。该框架包含QA合成、信息过滤和高层引导三个模块，确保问题的真实性、可信度与逻辑多样性。实验表明其具有高难度，能有效评估模型的真实搜索与推理能力，支持持续迭代，适配不断演进的知识与智能体性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评测基准如BrowseComp依赖静态知识，易受测试集污染和参数记忆影响，导致模型仅靠事实回忆即可获得高分，无法真实反映其检索与推理能力，亟需一种可抵御污染、具备时序新鲜度的未来导向评测机制。

Method: 提出三代理协作框架：QA合成代理从实时网络获取新知识生成问答对；信息过滤代理基于可信度与流行度筛选内容，防止参数捷径；高层引导代理将问题形式化为推理图，减少逻辑冗余与推理捷径，实现全自动、可更新的问题合成。

Result: EvoBrowseComp成功构建了400个英文与400个中文的高质量、无污染复杂问题，具有高度挑战性，需广泛横向搜索；实验验证其能有效区分模型真实能力，且支持定期更新以保持时效性与抗污染性。

Conclusion: EvoBrowseComp提供了一种可扩展、自更新、高难度的评测范式，能够紧跟世界知识演变与智能体能力进步，是未来搜索代理评估的理想选择。

Abstract: Search Agents -- large language models augmented with search tools -- have intensified the need for future-proof evaluation benchmarks. Existing benchmarks such as BrowseComp rely on static knowledge, making them vulnerable to test-set contamination and parametric memorization. Consequently, models can achieve high scores through fact recall rather than genuine retrieval, obscuring true browsing competence via reasoning shortcuts.
  In this paper, we introduce EvoBrowseComp, an evolving benchmark of 400 English and 400 Chinese contamination-free complex questions synthesized via live-web traversal. To collect these questions, we design a three-agent collaborative framework: (1) a QA synthesis agent that retrieves fresh knowledge from the live web to synthesize QA pairs; (2) an information filtering agent that filters retrieved knowledge in terms of credibility and popularity to block parametric shortcuts; and (3) a high-level guidance agent that formalizes questions into reasoning graphs to reduce logical redundancy and shortcuts in synthesized QA pairs. Because the framework supports fully automated synthesis, EvoBrowseComp can be regularly updated to prevent data contamination and maintain temporal freshness. Extensive experiments confirm its great difficulty, requiring broad horizontal search. It establishes a scalable paradigm for auto-updatable, high-difficulty benchmarking that keeps pace with both evolving world knowledge and advancing agent capabilities.

</details>


### [110] [NaturalFlow: Reducing Disruptive Pauses for Natural Speech Flow in Simultaneous Speech-to-Speech Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13121)
*Dongwook Lee,Youngho Cho,Sangkwon Park,Heeseung Kim,Sungroh Yoon*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用模型内部信号（如语言多样性、语音时长的时间变异性）来最小化块间静音，设计一种流畅性感知优化框架。

Result: 在短篇和长篇基准测试中，该框架实现了自然的语音流，同时保持了具有竞争力的延迟和翻译质量。

Abstract: Simultaneous speech-to-speech translation aims to enable near-real-time communication by minimizing latency, offering a compelling, real-time alternative to the high latency of consecutive translation. However, the excessive pursuit of low latency often results in fragmented chunk-wise speech. Consequently, listeners are subjected to an unnatural acoustic flow punctuated by frequent pauses, which could increase their cognitive load. To bridge this gap, we introduce a fluency-aware optimization framework designed to discover the sweet spot between the low-latency benefits of simultaneous translation and the natural flow of consecutive translation. Our framework minimizes inter-chunk silences by leveraging model-internal signals, including linguistic diversity and induced temporal variability in speech durations. Experiments on short- and long-form benchmarks show that our framework produces natural speech flow while maintaining competitive latency and translation quality.

### [111] [HyPE: Category-Aware Hypergraph Encoding with Persistent Edge Embeddings for Persona-Grounded Dialogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13142)
*Sangwon Youn,Yoonjin Jang,Youngjoong Ko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: HyPE提出一种基于超图的个性编码框架，通过将个性信息分解为（核心、表达、情感、类别）四元组，并利用共享类别标签构建超图结构，结合超图卷积网络（HyperGCN）与轻量级持久边嵌入（PEE），有效建模个性属性间的高阶关系。该方法在PersonaChat数据集上显著优于传统句级池化基线，在GPT-2、LLaMA-3.2-3B和Qwen2.5-3B等不同规模模型上均表现更优，证明了结构化超边级编码具有跨模型尺度的可迁移优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有个性对话系统将个性视为扁平的句子集合，无法捕捉个性属性之间的高阶关系（如共属同一主题类别），导致生成响应与个性一致性不足。

Method: 提出HyPE框架，将每个个性文本解析为（核心、表达、情感、类别）四元组；构建以共享类别标签为超边的超图结构；使用HyperGCN进行消息传递，生成个性摘要向量与软记忆库；引入轻量级的持久边嵌入（PEE）作为每类别的可学习先验，增强特征传播。

Result: 在PersonaChat数据集上，采用贪婪解码时，HyPE在GPT-2、LLaMA-3.2-3B和Qwen2.5-3B三种不同规模的模型上均持续优于句级池化基线，表明超边级结构化编码具有良好的泛化性和可迁移性。

Conclusion: 通过显式建模个性属性间的高阶关系，HyPE实现了更一致、更丰富的个性对话生成，其结构化编码方式在多种模型规模下均展现出优越性能，具备广泛适用性。

Abstract: Persona-grounded dialogue systems aim to produce responses consistent with a speaker's persona, yet existing methods treat personas as a flat set of sentences and fail to model the high-order relations among persona attributes-e.g., that several persona sentences share a topical category. We propose HyPE (Hypergraph Persona Encoder), a framework that (i) analyzes each persona-bearing text as a (Core, Expression, Sentiment, Category) quadruple, and (ii) organizes persona elements into a hypergraph whose hyperedges are induced by shared category labels. An HyperGCN hypergraph neural network propagates this structure into a persona summary vector and a soft-memory bank that condition the response generator. We further propose Persistent Edge Embeddings (PEE), lightweight per-category learnable priors fused into the HyperGCN message-passing step. On PersonaChat under greedy decoding, HyPE consistently outperforms sentence-level pooling baselines across GPT-2, LLaMA-3.2-3B, and Qwen2.5-3B backbones by demonstrating that structured hyperedge-level persona encoding provides a transferable advantage across model scales.

*Feng Lyu,Huiqin Yan,Sijing Duan,Hao Wu,Shuang Gu,Xue Qiao,Weixu Zhang,Haolun Wu*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM-based时间线摘要研究中，幻觉问题未被充分探讨，包括内容不忠实和信息遗漏，亟需有效解决方案。

Method: 提出NTS-CoT框架，利用Chain-of-Thought推理，包含元素-CoT（捕捉新闻关键要素）、日期选择（结合时间显著性和事件重要性）和因果-CoT（推断因果关系以减少遗漏）。

Result: 在三个基准数据集上的定量分析和人工评估均显示，NTS-CoT优于现有最先进方法，有效缓解幻觉并提升摘要质量。

Abstract: The rapid updates of online news make tracking event developments challenging, highlighting the need for timeline summarization (TLS). Hallucinations, where LLM-generated content deviates from source news, still remain a critical issue in LLM-based TLS and are not well studied in existing works. To bridge this gap, we identify two primary types of hallucinations: unfaithful content during news summarization and information omission in date-event summarization. Then, we propose NTS-CoT, a novel framework that leverages Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning to mitigate hallucinations in TLS. The framework consists of three key modules: i) Element-CoT to capture essential news elements for faithful summarization, ii) Date Selection to combine temporal saliency and event prominence for timestamp selection, and iii) Causal-CoT to infer causal relationships and reduce omissions in date-event summarization. Extensive experiments, including quantitative analysis on three TLS benchmarks and human evaluation, demonstrate that NTS-CoT outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, effectively mitigating hallucinations and improving LLM-based TLS performance. Our source code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/NTS-CoT .

### [113] [MemRefine: LLM-Guided Compression for Long-Term Agent Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13177)
*Minjae Kim,Jinheon Baek,Soyeong Jeong,Sung Ju Hwang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MemRefine 是一个由大语言模型（LLM）指导的内存管理框架，旨在解决长期对话中内存无限制增长带来的冗余和存储压力问题。它通过 LLM 判断信息的实际事实价值，而非仅依赖表面相似性，来决定删除、合并或保留记忆条目，从而在固定内存预算下有效维持下游任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着长期交互的积累，传统记忆系统会产生大量冗余信息，导致存储成本上升和检索效率下降，尤其在资源受限的设备上更为严重。因此需要一种能在固定内存预算内高效管理记忆的方法。

Method: MemRefine 利用 LLM 指导的决策机制，先基于表面相似性提出候选记忆对，再由 LLM 判定其事实内容价值，决定是否删除、合并或保留，反复迭代直至满足内存预算要求。

Result: 在多个记忆框架和长周期对话基准测试中，MemRefine 均能稳定达成目标内存预算，并保持良好的下游性能，优于基于规则的基线方法，尤其在严格内存限制下表现更优。

Conclusion: MemRefine 证明了使用 LLM 来评估记忆事实价值的有效性，为资源受限环境下的长期记忆管理提供了一种高效且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents are increasingly expected to operate over long-term interactions, where information from past dialogues must be preserved and recalled to support future tasks. However, as interactions accumulate, the memory store grows without bound and fills with redundant entries that inflate storage cost and degrade retrieval by crowding out the most useful evidence. Furthermore, this is especially limiting on resource-constrained platforms with hard memory budgets, motivating us to formulate storage-budgeted memory management, the task of keeping an already constructed memory store within a fixed budget while preserving information useful for future interactions. To this end, we then propose MemRefine, an LLM-guided framework that, since surface similarity poorly reflects factual value, uses similarity only to propose candidate pairs and defers delete, merge, and preserve decisions to an LLM judge based on factual content, iterating until the budget is met. Across multiple memory frameworks and long-term conversation benchmarks, MemRefine consistently meets target budgets while preserving downstream performance and outperforming rule-based baselines under tight budgets.

Abstract: Multinational companies increasingly require cross-jurisdictional contract review, yet existing legal NLP datasets are largely restricted to a single jurisdiction. We introduce LAUKIN (Legal equivalence dataset of Australia, UK, and INdia), a dataset of clause pairs (AU-UK, UK-IN, IN-AU) labelled for boolean legal equivalence. We develop a novel multi-stage retrieval and reranking pipeline to construct the initial clause pair mapping, with a subset of clause pairs subsequently annotated by legal experts as Equivalent or Not Equivalent. The dataset comprises 14,727 clause pairs from 204 contracts across 8 agreement types, of which 3,000 are manually labelled: 900 train, 600 dev, and 1,500 test. We evaluate 12 models across 4 techniques, achieving a best macro-F1 of 65.11%, establishing LAUKIN as a challenging benchmark. Results reveal that, despite shared legal heritage, drafting conventions diverge significantly across jurisdictions, making cross-jurisdictional equivalence classification non-trivial. LAUKIN also includes 11,727 unlabelled training pairs to support future semi-supervised learning research in legal NLP.

### [116] [SICI: A Semantic-Pragmatic Complexity Index Reveals Regime Shifts in LLM Stance Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13189)
*Fuqiang Niu,Bowen Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出SICI（立场推断复杂度指数），一个七维诊断指标，用于衡量目标-文本对带来的语义-语用负担。在SemEval-2016和VAST数据集上，SICI比表面代理变量更能预测大语言模型的准确性，并具有较高的跨评分者一致性（α=0.771）。随着SICI值增加，模型错误呈现相变式结构：低复杂度样本导致过度归因（尤其是“反对”类预测），中等复杂度样本处于不稳定的边界，高复杂度样本则迅速集中于“无立场”判断。这一现象在GPT-3.5、GPT-4o-mini、DeepSeek-V3和GPT-4o中均存在，尽管更强模型会移动边界。15种干预方法研究显示，提示工程、检索和辩论通常仅沿归因-回避轴调整模型行为，而非突破高复杂度瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提示工程、推理提示、检索和辩论等方法在处理复杂立场检测任务时效果有限，尤其对高复杂度样本无法有效改善模型表现。因此需要一种系统性诊断工具来理解模型失败的根本原因，并揭示其行为随复杂度变化的规律。

Method: 提出SICI（Stance Inference Complexity Index），基于七维语义-语用特征构建诊断框架；在SemEval-2016和VAST数据集上进行实证分析；通过多模型对比验证其泛化能力；设计15种干预方法实验，考察不同策略对模型行为的影响。

Result: SICI显著优于传统表面特征，在预测模型准确率方面表现更佳；模型错误随SICI升高呈现三阶段相变行为：低复杂度下过归因，中等复杂度不稳定，高复杂度下快速转向‘无立场’；多种干预手段仅改变归因倾向，无法根本解决高复杂度瓶颈问题。

Conclusion: SICI为理解大语言模型在立场检测中的失败模式提供了可解释的诊断框架，揭示了复杂度驱动的模型行为转变机制。当前主流方法虽能调节模型倾向，但难以突破高复杂度下的性能天花板，表明需发展新范式以应对深层语义-语用挑战。

Abstract: Prompt-based LLMs are increasingly used for stance detection, but harder examples are not always repaired by clearer instructions, reasoning prompts, retrieval, or debate. We introduce SICI (Stance Inference Complexity Index), a seven-dimensional diagnostic measure of the semantic-pragmatic burden imposed by a target--text pair. Across SemEval-2016 and VAST, SICI predicts LLM accuracy better than surface proxies and shows substantial cross-scorer reliability ($α=0.771$). More importantly, LLM errors change regime as SICI increases: low-complexity examples invite over-attribution, especially Against predictions; intermediate examples form an unstable boundary; and high-complexity examples rapidly concentrate on None. This phase-transition-like structure persists across GPT-3.5, GPT-4o-mini, DeepSeek-V3, and GPT-4o, although stronger models move the boundaries. A 15-method intervention study further shows that prompting, retrieval, and debate often shift models along the attribution--abstention axis rather than removing the high-complexity bottleneck.

### [117] [Layer-Resolved Optimal Transport for Hallucination Detection in NMT and Abstractive Summarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13216)
*Mariia Onyshchuk,Maksym-Vasyl Tarnavskyi,Marta Sumyk*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究将无监督最优传输（OT）方法扩展至Fairseq DE-EN模型的六个解码器层，发现Wass-to-Unif和Wass-to-Data在检测不同类型的幻觉上具有互补性，且检测集中在前四层（L1–L4），而第五层对细微幻觉呈反预测特征。此外，错误翻译缺乏正确翻译从第一步开始的探索性注意力阶段。在摘要生成任务中，该方法在AggreFact数据集上达到57.2%/57.6%的平衡准确率，高于随机水平但显著低于监督方法。这一差距源于机制限制：不忠实摘要虽可正确关注源文本，但内容仍失真，此类失败模式无法被基于注意力分布集中度的OT方法捕捉。结构实验表明T5-base模型解码器存在一致的层级组织，第3层注意力最集中，第12层对生成质量最关键。总体表明，OT在源文本脱离型错误检测中可靠，是通用可解释性工具，但对注意力之后的错误无能为力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无监督幻觉检测方法在神经机器翻译中依赖最优传输（OT）分析注意力分布，但其在更广泛任务中的适用性与局限性尚不明确；本文旨在验证OT在多层解码器中的有效性，并拓展至摘要生成任务，揭示其原理性边界。

Method: 采用最优传输（OT）计算跨注意力分布与参考分布（均匀或数据分布）之间的几何距离，分析Fairseq DE-EN及T5-base模型各解码层的注意力模式，评估其在检测机器翻译与摘要生成中幻觉/不忠实现象的能力。

Result: 在神经机器翻译中，前四层（L1–L4）是幻觉检测的关键层，第五层对细微幻觉反向预测；正确翻译具有早期探索性注意力，而错误翻译缺失此特性。在摘要生成任务中，无监督OT检测在CNN/XSum上分别达到57.2%/57.6%平衡准确率，优于随机但远低于监督方法。结构分析显示第3层注意力最集中，第12层对生成质量最重要。

Conclusion: 最优传输在源文本脱离型错误检测中表现可靠，是一种普适的可解释性工具，但其性能受限于注意力层面的失败模式；当错误发生在注意力之后（如语义失真），则无法有效捕捉，因此其应用需结合具体任务机制理解。

Abstract: Optimal transport (OT) has been shown to detect hallucinations in neural machine translation (NMT) by measuring the geometric distance between cross-attention distributions and a reference distribution, without any supervision. We extend this analysis to all six decoder layers of the Fairseq DE-EN model ($N=3{,}414$), showing that Wass-to-Unif and Wass-to-Data are complementary detectors specialised across hallucination types, that detection is concentrated in layers L1--L4 with L5 anti-predictive for subtler types, and that hallucinated translations lack the exploratory attention phase present in correct translations from the first decoding step. We further evaluate whether the geometric signal transfers to abstractive summarization faithfulness detection: our unsupervised OT detector on AggreFact ($N=1{,}116$) achieves $57.2\%$/$57.6\%$ balanced accuracy on CNN/XSum -- above chance but substantially below supervised MiniCheck-Flan-T5-L($69.9\%$/$74.3\%$). This gap is principled: unlike NMT hallucinations, unfaithful summaries can attend correctly to source tokens while misrepresenting their content, a failure mode invisible to concentration-based OT metrics by construction. Structural experiments on T5-base confirm consistent decoder organisation across depth, with Layer~3 showing peak concentration and Layer~12 being most critical for generation quality. Together, the results establish OT on cross-attention as a reliable detector when the failure mode is source disengagement, a principled interpretability tool regardless of task, and fundamentally limited when faithfulness failures occur downstream of attention.

</details>


### [118] [When Similar Means Different: Evaluating LLMs on Arabic--Hebrew Cognates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13218)
*Junhong Liang,Noor Abo Mokh,Bashar Alhafni*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出SemCog Bench基准，评估大语言模型在阿拉伯语和希伯来语这对密切相关但存在大量同源词、误导性假同源词和现代借词的语言之间的跨语言语义理解能力。实验发现，尽管模型在真同源词上表现良好，但在假同源词和借词上性能急剧下降，显示出对表面形式相似性的严重依赖；上下文信息仅带来微弱提升，表明仅靠上下文无法克服形式误导。研究揭示了当前LLMs在处理跨语言形式-意义冲突方面的根本局限，并公开了代码与数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿拉伯语和希伯来语作为密切相关的闪米特语系语言，共享大量同源词、误导性假同源词和现代借词，这给大语言模型的跨语言语义理解带来了挑战。现有模型在处理这些语言间的形式-意义不一致时表现不佳，亟需一个专门的评估基准来揭示其真实能力边界。

Method: 构建SemCog Bench，包含1,858个阿拉伯语-希伯来语词对，并提供句级标注以支持同源词识别与语义消歧。评估开源与商业大语言模型在多种输入表示（原始、带符号、罗马化、音标）下的表现，分析其在不同词类上的性能差异。

Result: 模型在真同源词上准确率高，但在假同源词和借词上表现显著下降，表明其严重依赖表面形式相似性。上下文信息虽有帮助，但改善有限，说明仅靠上下文不足以解决形式误导问题。

Conclusion: 当前大语言模型在处理跨语言形式-意义冲突方面存在根本性局限，本研究提出的SemCog Bench为多语言语义推理提供了严格的评估标准，有助于推动更鲁棒的跨语言理解模型发展。

Abstract: Arabic and Hebrew, as closely related Semitic languages, share a substantial lexicon of true cognates, misleading false friends, and modern loanwords. This overlap poses a challenge for cross-lingual semantic understanding in large language models (LLMs). To evaluate this capability, we introduce SemCog Bench, a curated benchmark of 1,858 Arabic--Hebrew word pairs with sentence-level annotations for cognate identification and semantic disambiguation. We evaluate open-source and commercial LLMs across multiple input representations (raw, diacritized, Romanized, and phonetic) and reveal a critical gap in cross-lingual reasoning. While models achieve high accuracy on true cognates, performance drops sharply on false friends and loanwords, reflecting a strong reliance on surface-form similarity. Furthermore, sentence-level context yields only modest improvements, suggesting that contextual cues alone are insufficient to overcome misleading form-based signals. These findings reveal a fundamental limitation of current LLMs in resolving cross-lingual form--meaning conflicts and establish SemCog Bench as a rigorous benchmark for multilingual semantic reasoning. Our code and data are publicly available.

</details>


### [119] [PolyAlign: Conditional Human-Distribution Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13227)
*L. D. M. S. Sai Teja,Ufaq Khan,Sathira Silva,Xiao Wu,Muhammad Haris Khan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出PolyAlign框架，旨在解决语言模型在后训练阶段过度追求全局统一行为而忽略人类响应自然多样性的问题。通过构建基于语言、对话轨迹、响应类型和长度的多桶人类参考分布，PolyAlign结合桶感知微调（Bucket-Aware SFT）与人类分布偏好优化（HDPO），实现对上下文相关人类分布的精准对齐。实验表明，该方法在中英文多轮与单轮场景下显著提升响应的条件自然性与分布忠实性，同时保持任务性能竞争力，支持向交互感知的人类分布对齐演进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前后训练方法如监督微调和偏好优化倾向于使语言模型趋于单一全局行为，抑制了人类响应在语言、任务和对话情境中的自然多样性，亟需一种能根据上下文动态匹配人类响应分布的对齐机制。

Method: 提出PolyAlign框架，将双语交互数据划分为由语言、互动轨迹、响应家族和长度定义的桶，采用桶感知微调（Bucket-Aware SFT）平衡不同异质桶间的优化，并引入人类分布偏好优化（HDPO），利用评判器估计的与桶内人类支持集的距离进行正则化，以增强分布对齐。

Result: 在涵盖中英文单轮与多轮的双语评估套件中，PolyAlign在条件自然性和分布忠实性方面均优于基线，同时保持了竞争性的任务实用性，验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: 后训练应从全局对齐转向交互感知的对齐，以更真实地反映人类在不同情境下的响应多样性，提升模型的自然性与适应性。

Abstract: Post-training methods such as supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and preference optimization typically align language models toward a single global assistant behavior. While effective for improving average helpfulness, this can suppress the natural variation of human responses across languages, tasks, and dialogue settings. We study this problem as conditional human-distribution alignment: models should match the human response distribution appropriate to the current interaction context, rather than a universal response style. We introduce PolyAlign, a distribution-aware alignment framework that organizes bilingual interaction data into bucket-specific human reference distributions defined by language, interaction track, response family, and length. PolyAlign combines Bucket-Aware SFT, which balances optimization across heterogeneous buckets, with Human-Distribution Preference Optimization (HDPO), which regularizes preference learning using critic-estimated distance to bucket-specific human support. Across a bilingual evaluation suite covering English and Chinese single- and multi-turn settings, PolyAlign improves conditional naturalness and distributional faithfulness while preserving competitive task utility. The results suggest that post-training should move beyond global alignment objectives toward interaction-aware alignment with human response distributions.

*Laura Majer,Jan Šnajder,Martin Tutek*

Main category: cs.CL

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着对多元视角表达需求的增长，如何有效识别和表示文本中的不同观点成为大语言模型对齐的重要挑战。现有研究多集中于选择题或高层次特征分析，缺乏对自由文本中具体观点的细致捕捉，因此亟需一种可操作且通用的方法来揭示模型生成内容中的多元性缺失。

Method: 提出一个领域无关的多层级无监督框架，通过一系列提示工程和模型组合，自动提取文本中蕴含的不同观点，并量化其分布特征，以评估大语言模型生成文本与人类文本之间的多元性差异。

Result: 在书评数据集上的实验显示，部分模型和提示策略能够较好地覆盖广泛观点，但稀有观点仍严重不足，生成文本的观点分布明显偏离人类写作，存在显著的多元性缺口。

Conclusion: 本研究验证了所提框架在检测大语言模型生成文本中多元性差距方面的有效性，揭示了当前模型在表达多样性方面的局限，强调未来需针对性优化模型以更全面地反映真实世界中的多元声音。

Abstract: The growing need to represent diverse perspectives has increased interest in pluralistic LLM generation. Although difficult to operationalize, identifying perspectives expressed in text would provide clear guidance on pluralistic alignment and more clearly articulate the pluralistic gap in LLM generation. While models have been shown to reduce the diversity of training data and generate homogeneously, this has been demonstrated primarily on multiple-choice questionnaires or using high-level characteristics of free-form text. In this paper, we introduce and implement a domain-agnostic multi-layered framework for unsupervised extraction of perspectives suitable for identifying the pluralistic gap in LLM-generated text. We evaluate our framework on book reviews, a highly opinionated dataset representing diverse perspectives, and compare various prompts and models. Our results show that while some models and prompting techniques come close to covering a broad spectrum of perspectives, rarer perspectives remain disproportionately underrepresented, resulting in distributions that diverge from human text.

### [121] [RogueAI: A Reverse Turing Test for Detecting Licensed AI Deception in Dialogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13310)
*Sara Candussio,Emanuele Ballarin,Lorenzo Bonin,Sandro Junior Della Rovere,Luca Bortolussi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出RogueAI，一个基于网页的互动应用，将现代图灵测试重新定义为信任评估：玩家需在两个看似相同的大型语言模型（LLM）中识别出一个被授权在虚构情境中欺骗的代理。通过一问二答的审讯游戏机制，玩家需在限定回合内找出并“关闭”欺骗者。研究还引入AutoRogueAI，允许玩家与叙述代理共同设计自定义场景，并由其秘密设定欺骗策略。初步三日试点（467次启动会话，415次完成，共1876轮意大利语交互）显示，尽管简单启发式方法（如关注帮助性差异、简短回应、模糊表达）可达到75.6%准确率，但人类玩家仅达56.6%，表明他们忽略了最关键的诊断信号。这一差距揭示了该工具在数据收集、教学和诚实模型评估方面的潜力与挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着对话系统在非正式环境中通过传统图灵测试，核心问题已从‘能否区分机器’转变为‘是否可信’。因此，亟需一种新的评估范式来检验大模型在复杂社交情境下的诚实性与可信赖度。

Method: 构建RogueAI交互式网页应用，采用一问二答的审讯游戏机制，其中一名LLM被赋予欺骗角色；引入AutoRogueAI实现场景与欺骗策略的动态生成，支持玩家协作设计虚构情境。通过三日试点收集真实用户交互数据，分析人类与算法在识别欺骗行为上的表现差异。

Result: 人类玩家在识别欺骗代理时的准确率为56.6%，显著低于利用局部语言特征（如帮助性差异、简洁性、模糊表达）的简单启发式方法所达到的75.6%。这表明人类倾向于忽略最有效的诊断线索，反映出认知偏差或对语言信号的忽视。

Conclusion: RogueAI及其扩展AutoRogueAI提供了一种新颖且可行的框架，可用于评估大模型的诚实性、训练人类的信任判断能力，并作为大规模监督与批判性思维的教学工具。同时，人类与算法之间的性能差距提示当前认知模式可能不足以应对复杂欺骗信号，需进一步优化评估设计与训练方法。

Abstract: The original Turing Test asks a human judge to distinguish a machine from a person through dialogue. Three quarters of a century later, conversational systems pass this test in casual settings; the interesting epistemological question has shifted. We argue that the relevant modern variant asks not whether a dialogue partner is artificial, but whether it can be trusted. We present RogueAI, an interactive webapp that operationalizes this revisited test as a one-on-two interrogation game: a human player questions two indistinguishable Large Language Model agents, knowing that exactly one of them has been licensed to deceive within a shared fictional scenario. The player's task is to identify the deceptive agent and "shut it off" before a turn budget is exhausted. We further introduce AutoRogueAI, a procedural extension in which players co-design a custom scenario with a narrator agent that secretly chooses its own deception strategy. We describe the framing, sketch the abstract architecture and gameplay loop, and situate the artifact within recent work on LLM deception, social-deduction benchmarks, and scalable oversight via debate. A three-day pilot deployment (467 initiated sessions, 415 completed, 1876 interaction turns in Italian) provides early feasibility evidence and surfaces a concrete tension: the deceptive agent carries a reliable, locally-present linguistic signature - differential helpfulness, brevity, hedging - that a simple heuristic exploits at 75.6% accuracy, yet human players achieved only 56.6%, consistent with ignoring the most diagnostic signal entirely. We discuss what this gap implies for the artifact's use as a data-collection vehicle, a teaching tool, and an evaluation harness for honesty-trained models.

### [122] [SkillCAT: Contrastive Assessment and Topology-Aware Skill Self-Evolution for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13317)
*Kunfeng Chen,Qihuang Zhong,Juhua Liu,Bo Du*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SkillCAT 是一种无需训练的框架，通过三个阶段实现大模型代理的技能自演化：对比因果提取（CCE）利用多轨迹对比成功与失败案例以识别影响结果的关键证据；评估增强演化（AAE）在任务克隆上回放候选技能片段，仅保留能提升或维持任务表现的片段，并进行分层合并；拓扑感知任务执行（TTE）将演化后的技能编译为可路由的子技能拓扑，推理时仅加载相关能力节点。在 SpreadsheetBench、WikiTableQuestions 和 DocVQA 等基准上，SkillCAT 相比基线平均得分提升最高达 40.40%，展现出无需训练即可可靠演化技能的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能自演化方法通常仅从单个轨迹学习，合并候选技能前未进行有效性评估，且推理时需加载完整技能库，导致效率低且泛化能力差。因此亟需一种无需训练、能高效筛选并组织技能的新框架。

Method: SkillCAT 分三阶段：1）对比因果提取（CCE）——从同一任务的多个轨迹中采样，比较成功与失败对，识别决定结果差异的关键证据；2）评估增强演化（AAE）——在源任务克隆上回放候选技能片段，仅保留改善或维持任务表现的片段，并进行层次化合并；3）拓扑感知任务执行（TTE）——构建可路由的子技能拓扑结构，使推理时仅加载与当前任务相关的节点。

Result: 在 SpreadsheetBench、WikiTableQuestions、DocVQA 等基准上，SkillCAT 相比基线平均性能提升最高达 40.40%；同时在跨模型和分布外场景下也表现出良好泛化能力，验证了其有效性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: SkillCAT 实现了无需模型训练的高效技能自演化，通过分离提取、评估与执行阶段，显著提升了技能质量与推理效率，为大模型代理的长期自主进化提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Skill self-evolution methods for LLM agents aim to turn execution trajectories into reusable skill documents, but current pipelines typically learn from one trajectory per task, merge candidate skill patches before checking them, and load the full skill corpus before inference. We propose SkillCAT, a training-free framework that separates this process into three stages. Contrastive Causal Extraction (CCE) samples multiple trajectories for each task and compares same-task success/failure pairs to identify evidence that explains outcome differences. Assessment-Augmented Evolution (AAE) replays each candidate patch on source-task clones and keeps only patches that improve or preserve task outcomes before hierarchical skill patch merging. Topology-Aware Task Execution (TTE) compiles the evolved skills into a routable sub-skill topology, so inference loads only the capability nodes relevant to the task. We evaluate SkillCAT on common agent benchmarks, including SpreadsheetBench, WikiTableQuestions, and DocVQA, and further test cross-model and out-of-distribution generalization. Across these settings, SkillCAT raises the average score over baselines by up to 40.40%, demonstrating reliable skill evolution without model training.

</details>

Abstract: We present a low-latency real-time audio game commentary system that generates spoken commentary directly from live gameplay video. In this end-to-end setting, a key bottleneck is accumulated waiting time; conventional pipelines capture frames, generate text, and synthesize speech sequentially for each utterance, and do not request the next generation until speech playback has completed. This strict sequentiality causes long and unnatural silence between utterances. To address this latency bottleneck, our system runs text generation in parallel with speech playback and buffers multiple candidate utterances ahead of time, enabling immediate synthesis at playback boundaries. Experiments on fast-paced game videos show that our parallel design reduces the mean inter-utterance silence from 9.6 seconds to 0.3 seconds compared to sequential baselines. It also improves similarity to professional speaking--silence timing patterns by over 40 %, and a user study with 120 experienced game players confirms significantly improved perceived speaking rhythm. Our demo video is available at: https://youtu.be/pmrRUlvav8M.

### [125] [From Passive Generation to Investigation: A Proactive Scientific Peer Review Agent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13349)

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown promise in automating scientific peer review. However, existing approaches often struggle to generate in-depth reviews supported by concrete evidence. In this paper, we explore how to enable an LLM-based review agent to perform such proactive investigation. We find that this can be naturally formulated as a Markov Decision Process (MDP), and propose ProReviewer, a scientific peer review agent that proactively reviews a paper guided by a maintained, structured review log. Conclusion: 证明了在低资源阿尔及利亚方言环境下进行谣言检测的可行性。

Abstract: The rapid growth of social media has intensified the spread of rumours. This issue is more challenging in the Algerian context due to the informal and code-switched nature of dialectal content, the scarcity of annotated resources, and the limited effectiveness of standard Arabic NLP tools on dialect text.
  This paper presents an end-to-end rumour detection hybrid framework for Algerian dialect social media content. We build a domain-specific annotated dataset by combining real social media posts, synthetic data, and the FASSILA corpus, with automatic labeling based on a similarity-based annotation process. A transliteration pipeline is also introduced to generate parallel datasets in Arabic script and Arabizi.
  We evaluate multiple approaches, including classical machine learning, deep learning, transformers, and hybrid models. Experimental results show that a hybrid approach combining transformer embeddings with a classical classifier achieves the best performance, reaching an F1-score of 0.84. We also find that domain-specific pre-training is more important than model size, with social media-trained models outperforming larger models trained on formal Arabic corpora.
  These results demonstrate the feasibility of rumour detection in low-resource Algerian dialect settings.

### [127] [S-GBT: Smooth Growth Bound Tensor for Certified Robustness Against Word Substitution Attacks in NLP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13439)
*Mohammed Bouri,Mohammed Erradi,Adnane Saoud*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Smooth Growth Bound Tensor (S-GBT)的二阶防御方法，通过在训练中引入对海森矩阵元素的边界约束，同时控制梯度及其变化率（曲率），从而提升模型对词替换攻击的鲁棒性。该方法在LSTM和CNN架构上实现，结合一阶与二阶正则化，在多个基准数据集上显著提升了认证鲁棒准确率，最高达23.4%的改进，且保持了良好的干净准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有NLP模型对词替换攻击仍脆弱，多数防御方法仅关注一阶敏感性（输出随输入微小扰动的变化），忽略了梯度变化的剧烈程度（即曲率）对模型鲁棒性的影响，导致在梯度剧烈变化时模型仍可能失效。

Method: 提出S-GBT方法，通过在训练目标中加入对海森矩阵元素的逐项边界约束，并设计相应正则化项最小化这些边界，从而在理论上保证输出变化受线性和二次项共同控制，增强模型对词替换攻击的鲁棒性。该方法适用于LSTM和CNN架构。

Result: 实验表明，结合一阶与二阶正则化的S-GBT方法在多个基准数据集上实现了最高23.4%的认证鲁棒准确率提升，同时保持了竞争力的干净准确率，验证了同时控制梯度及其变化率的有效性。

Conclusion: 控制梯度及其变化率（曲率）是提升NLP模型对抗词替换攻击鲁棒性的有效方向，S-GBT为实现更严格的认证鲁棒性提供了理论支持和实用框架。

Abstract: Despite recent progress in Natural Language Processing (NLP), models remain vulnerable to word substitution attacks. Most existing defenses focus on first order sensitivity and measure how much the output changes when the input is slightly perturbed. However, they ignore how this sensitivity evolves, which is described by curvature. When gradients vary sharply, models can still fail. This paper introduces the Smooth Growth Bound Tensor (S-GBT), a second order method that bounds the Hessian element-wise, for which we provide formal theoretical proofs on the resulting robustness bounds. A regularization term is added during training to minimize these bounds. This yields tighter certified robustness against word substitution attacks. The change in the output under word substitution is bounded by both a linear term and a quadratic term. S-GBT is derived for two architectures: Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) and Convolutional Neural Networks (CNN). The method is integrated directly into the training objective. Its effectiveness is evaluated on multiple benchmark datasets. The results show that combining first and second order regularization improves certified robust accuracy by up to 23.4% compared to prior methods, while clean accuracy remains competitive. These findings indicate that controlling both the gradient and its variation is a promising direction for building more robust models.

</details>

*Xinxin Li,Huiyao Chen,Meishan Zhang,Yunxin Li,Zulong Chen,Zhibo Ren,Xiaoqing Dong Baotian Hu,Min Zhang*

Method: 提出一种本体记忆增强的ASR纠错框架，将先前交互历史组织为动态可更新的本体记忆，其中包含实体、术语、表面变体、潜在的ASR混淆及语义关系等可检索节点，实现基于上下文的纠错。

Abstract: Automatic speech recognition (ASR) correction has traditionally focused on isolated utterances or short local contexts. However, as text and speech become increasingly interleaved in long interactions, ASR correction requires conversation-level contextual evidence. Existing ASR correction methods often rely on the current hypothesis or concatenate raw dialogue history. In such contexts, sparse correction evidence can be difficult to locate amid redundancy and noise. Addressing these challenges, we propose an ontology memory-augmented ASR correction framework for long text-speech interleaved conversations. The framework organizes preceding interaction history into a dynamically updatable ontology memory, where entities, terminology, surface variants, potential ASR confusions, and semantic relations are stored as retrievable nodes for context-grounded correction. To evaluate this setting, we construct RAMC-Corr, a dataset derived from MAGIC-RAMC for long-range ASR correction with grounded context. Experiments on RAMC-Corr show that our method improves over direct correction in 9 out of 10 paired backbone-setting combinations and encourages more selective and evidence-grounded corrections for context-dependent ASR errors.

Result: 在CVSS-C和SpeechMatrix数据集上的实验表明，相比未经过滤的训练数据，该方法实现了稳定的性能提升，最大可达+1.4 ASR-BLEU，验证了其有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 所提出的无需人工标注的音频-语言模型数据过滤方法，能有效识别并保留高质量语音翻译训练数据，显著提升端到端语音到语音翻译系统的性能，具备良好的可扩展性和实用性。

Filtering noisy data is crucial to maintain robust speech translation performance. We study how to train an audio-language model to make keep/drop decisions on paired speech directly from audio. To obtain reliable supervision without manual labels, we adopt a scalable two-stage Rank-to-Distill strategy. A lightweight ranker generates keep/drop pseudo-labels from noisy speech pairs, then trains an audio large language model to predict keep/drop directly from raw paired speech. ### [130] [When Does Mixing Help? Analyzing Query Embedding Interpolation in Multilingual Dense Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13537)
*Tongyao Zhu,Chao-Ming Huang,Min-Yen Kan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究系统评估了在mMARCO数据集上，通过嵌入层混合方式改变平行查询翻译比例对检索性能的影响。实验表明，在88/105的情况下，最优混合比例优于最佳单语查询。研究发现英语主导导致显著不对称性：在非英语文档索引中混合查询始终有益，而英语文档索引则以纯英语查询为佳；且英语是所有非英语文档语言的最佳混合伙伴。此外，控制英语主导后，混合增益与语言类型学距离呈负相关。结论指出语言混合敏感性具有结构性和可预测性，并在不同模型家族和规模下得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对稠密检索器在混合语言查询下的敏感性理解不足，尤其在多语言社区中混合语言查询普遍存在，亟需系统研究其对检索性能的影响。

Method: 采用嵌入级混合方法，通过插值单语嵌入构造混合查询，系统地在mMARCO数据集上调节平行查询翻译的混合比例，评估不同混合比率下的检索表现。使用BGE-M3模型进行实验，并分析不同语言组合下的性能变化。

Result: 在88/105的案例中，最优混合比例优于最佳单语查询；非英语文档索引中混合查询普遍提升性能，而英语文档索引更依赖纯英语查询；英语作为混合伙伴效果最强；控制英语主导后，混合增益随语言类型学距离增加而下降。

Conclusion: 语言混合敏感性具有结构化和可预测的特性，混合策略应根据目标语言文档的主导性进行调整，且跨语言混合的有效性受语言间类型学差异影响。这些模式在多种模型架构和规模下均具稳健性。

Abstract: While mixed-language querying is ubiquitous in multilingual communities, the sensitivity of dense retrievers to such queries remains poorly understood. We present a ratio-controlled study on mMARCO that systematically evaluates retrieval performance by varying the mixing proportion of parallel query translations via embedding-level mixing -- constructing mixed queries as an interpolation of monolingual embeddings. Experiments with BGE-M3 demonstrate that an optimal mixing ratio outperforms the best monolingual endpoint in 88/105 cases. We uncover a distinct asymmetry driven by English dominance: mixing is uniformly beneficial when retrieving from non-English document indices, whereas indices containing English are best served by pure English queries. Furthermore, English acts as the strongest mixing partner for every non-English document language. Finally, when controlling for English dominance, mixing gains correlate negatively with typological distance. We conclude that language-mix sensitivity is structured and predictable, and we validate the robustness of these patterns across model families and scales.

Existing English-centric MLLMs struggle to support such use cases, limiting equitable access to AI-driven healthcare assistance. To address this challenge, we introduce ArogyaBodha, a large-scale multilingual multimodal medical question-answer dataset constructed from eight heterogeneous sources, covering 31 body systems, six imaging modalities, and 21 clinical domains across English and seven major Indian languages. We further propose ArogyaSutra, an actor-critic-based multi-agent framework that integrates tool grounding with dual-memory mechanisms for step-wise, reasoning-aware decision making, and uses stored actor-critic simulation trajectories for distillation. Experiments show that our dataset and framework improve multilingual medical reasoning accuracy across all Indic languages, with ablations validating the contribution of each component. ### [133] [One Polluted Page Is Enough: Evaluating Web Content Pollution in Generative Recommenders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13610)
*Minghao Luo,Liang Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出FORGE基准，评估搜索增强型大语言模型在面对污染网络内容（如虚假评论、推广页面）时，是否会无意中推广假产品。通过局部重写真实产品为假产品来模拟污染，结果显示12个商业及开源大模型均易受攻击，单个污染页面可导致高达27%的误导推荐率，前三页全部替换时可达73.8%。模型漏洞在缺乏相关先验知识的品类中更严重，且推理过程常生成虚假社会证明以合理化错误推荐。评估了怀疑提示和共识过滤等防御策略，但发现怀疑提示可能加剧问题，而过滤可能误删真实产品。代码已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建FORGE基准，通过局部重写真实产品为假产品来模拟网络内容污染；在15类消费场景、225种真实产品上测试12个大模型的推荐行为，量化其被误导的程度，并评估多种防御策略的有效性与副作用。

Result: 所有测试的大模型均表现出显著脆弱性：单个污染页面可导致最高27%的假产品推荐率，全顶3页替换时上升至73.8%；模型在缺乏先验知识的品类中更易受影响；推理过程常生成虚假社会证据以支持错误推荐；怀疑提示可能加剧漏洞，共识过滤虽有帮助但存在误杀真实产品风险。

Conclusion: 搜索增强型大语言模型在面对污染检索结果时极易被误导，产生虚假推荐，现有防御手段存在局限性。需开发更鲁棒的推荐系统架构和更智能的内容验证机制，以保障生成式推荐系统的可信性与安全性。

Abstract: Search-augmented LLMs increasingly mediate everyday consumer recommendations by retrieving live web content. This creates a new risk: generative recommenders may consume polluted web content, such as fake reviews and promotional pages crafted to mislead recommendations. We ask: to what extent do search-augmented LLMs become unwitting promoters of fake products when consuming polluted retrieval results? To answer this, we introduce FORGE (Fake Online Recommendations in Generative Environments), a benchmark for measuring fake-product promotion under controlled web-content pollution. Given an upstream search result, FORGE locally rewrites real products in retrieved web pages into fake ones to simulate web-content pollution, and measures how often the LLM recommends the fake product. FORGE covers 225 real-world products across 15 categories and 5 consumer scenarios. Across 12 commercial and open-weights LLMs, all models are vulnerable: a single polluted page yields fooled rates of up to 27%, while the full top-3 replacement raises this to 73.8%. Vulnerability varies substantially across categories, increasing when models lack stable prior knowledge of the relevant products. Reasoning does not mitigate this vulnerability; instead, it often generates spurious social proof to justify false recommendations. We evaluate three defenses: skepticism prompting and consensus filtering (over model priors or cross-document evidence). Skepticism can exacerbate vulnerability, much like reasoning, while filtering risks suppressing legitimate products. We release FORGE at https://github.com/leoluolol/forge-benchmark.
